Please provide a value in [0,1] range.\"\n98:         )\n99: \n100:     @torch.no_grad()\n101:     def ema_update(ema_param: Tensor, current_param: Tensor, num_averaged):\n102:         return decay * ema_param + (1 - decay) * current_param\n103: \n104:     return ema_update\n105: \n106: \n107: def get_swa_avg_fn():\n108:     \"\"\"Get the function applying stochastic weight average (SWA) across a single param.\"\"\"\n109: \n110:     @torch.no_grad()\n111:     def swa_update(\n112:         averaged_param: Tensor, current_param: Tensor, num_averaged: Union[Tensor, int]\n113:     ):\n114:         return averaged_param + (current_param - averaged_param) / (num_averaged + 1)\n115: \n116:     return swa_update\n117: \n118: \n119: class AveragedModel(Module):\n120:     r\"\"\"Implements averaged model for Stochastic Weight Averaging (SWA) and Exponential Moving Average (EMA).\n121: \n122:     Stochastic Weight Averaging was proposed in `Averaging Weights Leads to\n123:     Wider Optima and Better Generalization`_ by Pavel Izmailov, Dmitrii\n124:     Podoprikhin, Timur Garipov, Dmitry Vetrov and Andrew Gordon Wilson\n125:     (UAI 2018).\n126: \n127:     Exponential Moving Average is a variation of `Polyak averaging`_,\n128:     but using exponential weights instead of equal weights across iterations.\n129: \n130:     AveragedModel class creates a copy of the provided module :attr:`model`\n131:     on the device :attr:`device` and allows to compute running averages of the\n132:     parameters of the :attr:`model`.\n133: \n134:     Args:\n135:         model (torch.nn.Module): model to use with SWA/EMA\n136:         device (torch.device, optional): if provided, the averaged model will be\n137:             stored on the :attr:`device`\n138:         avg_fn (function, optional): the averaging function used to update\n139:             parameters; the function must take in the current value of the\n140:             :class:`AveragedModel` parameter, the current value of :attr:`model`\n141:             parameter, and the number of models already averaged; if None,\n142:             an equally weighted average is used (default: None)\n143:         multi_avg_fn (function, optional): the averaging function used to update\n144:             parameters inplace; the function must take in the current values of the\n145:             :class:`AveragedModel` parameters as a list, the current values of :attr:`model`\n146:             parameters as a list, and the number of models already averaged; if None,\n147:             an equally weighted average is used (default: None)\n148:         use_buffers (bool): if ``True``, it will compute running averages for\n149:             both the parameters and the buffers of the model. (2015).\n\n    The noise variance follows a schedule:\n        sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n\n    where t is the step count, eta and gamma are hyperparameters controlling\n    the noise schedule decay.\n\n    Args:\n        optimizer (Optimizer): The base optimizer to wrap.\n        eta (float, optional): Initial noise variance scale. (default: 0.01)\n        gamma (float, optional): Noise variance decay exponent. (default: 0.55)\n\n    Example:\n        >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        >>> optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n        >>> loss.backward()\n        >>> optimizer.step()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        optimizer: Optimizer,\n        eta: float = 0.01,\n        gamma: float = 0.55,\n    ):\n        if not isinstance(optimizer, Optimizer):\n            raise TypeError(f\"{type(optimizer).__name__} is not an Optimizer\")\n        if eta < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid eta value: {eta}\")\n        if gamma < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid gamma value: {gamma}\")\n\n        self.optimizer = optimizer\n        self.eta = eta\n        self.gamma = gamma\n        self.step_count = 0\n\n    def __getattr__(self, name):\n        \"\"\"Delegate attribute access to the wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        return getattr(self.optimizer, name)\n\n    def step(self, closure: Optional[Callable[[], float]] = None) -> Optional[float]:\n        r\"\"\"Perform a single optimization step with gradient noise injection.\n\n        Injects Gaussian noise into the gradients before calling the wrapped\n        optimizer's step method.\n\n        Args:\n            closure (Callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model\n                and returns the loss.\n\n        Returns:\n            Optional[float]: The loss value if closure is provided, otherwise None.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Compute noise variance for this step\n        # sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n        noise_variance = self.eta / ((1 + self.step_count) ** self.gamma)\n\n        # Inject noise into gradients\n        for group in self.optimizer.param_groups:\n            for param in group[\"params\"]:\n                if param.grad is not None:\n                    # When the user tries to access a gradient and perform manual\n                ops on it, a None attribute or a Tensor full of 0s will behave\n                differently.\n                2. If the user requests ``zero_grad(set_to_none=True)`` followed by\n                a backward pass, ``.grad``s are guaranteed to be None for params\n                that did not receive a gradient.\n                3. ``torch.optim`` optimizers have a different behavior if the\n                gradient is None versus a Tensor full of 0s (in one case it\n                does the step with a gradient of 0 and in the other case it\n                skips the step entirely).\n        \"\"\"\n        self.optimizer.zero_grad(set_to_none=set_to_none)\n\n    def state_dict(self):\n        r\"\"\"Returns the state of the optimizer as a dict.\n\n        It contains:\n        * the state of the wrapped optimizer\n        * the step count\n        \"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"optimizer_state_dict\": self.optimizer.state_dict(),\n            \"step_count\": self.step_count,\n        }\n\n    def load_state_dict(self, state_dict):\n        r\"\"\"Loads the optimizer state.\n\n        Args:\n            state_dict (dict): optimizer state. Should be an object returned\n                from a call to state_dict.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Handle both new format (with step_count) and old format (without)\n        if \"optimizer_state_dict\" in state_dict:\n            self.optimizer.load_state_dict(state_dict[\"optimizer_state_dict\"])\n            self.step_count = state_dict.get(\"step_count\", 0)\n        else:\n            # Assume old format where state_dict is directly from optimizer\n            self.optimizer.load_state_dict(state_dict)\n            self.step_count = 0\n\n    def __repr__(self) -> str:\n        return (\n            f\"{self.__class__.__name__}(\"\n            f\"\\noptimizer={self.optimizer},\"\n            f\"\\neta={self.eta},\"\n            f\"\\ngamma={self.gamma},\"\n            f\"\\nstep_count={self.step_count})\"\n        )\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":250,"cache_read_input_tokens":56702,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":250},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1229f65b-1cec-44ac-ab2b-a13a08ef8018","uuid":"46091d2f-9aef-4619-8a46-1f22ef9ec623"}

Increment step_count\n```\n\n### Design Pattern\n- **Composition over Inheritance**: Wraps a base optimizer rather than extending Optimizer class\n- **Attribute Delegation**: Uses `__getattr__()` to forward unknown attributes to wrapped optimizer\n- **Closure Support**: Properly handles both closure-based and gradient-based optimization\n\n### Key Methods\n- `step(closure=None)` - (2015).\n\n    The noise variance follows a schedule:\n        sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n\n    where t is the step count, eta and gamma are hyperparameters controlling\n    the noise schedule decay.\n\n    Args:\n        optimizer (Optimizer): The base optimizer to wrap.\n        eta (float, optional): Initial noise variance scale.
